(**
 Properties of projection functions

 Contents:
 1. First projection is a Street fibration
 2. First projection is a Street opfibration
 *)

[notation-overridden,parsing,default]

[notation-overridden,parsing,default]

Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Core.Categories.
Require Import UniMath.Bicategories.Core.Bicat.
Import Bicat.Notations.
Require Import UniMath.Bicategories.Core.Invertible_2cells.
Require Import UniMath.Bicategories.Morphisms.InternalStreetFibration.

Import Products.Notations.

Local Open Scope cat.

(**
 1. First projection is a Street fibration
 *)
Section ProjectionSFib.
  Context {B : bicat_with_binprod}
          (b₁ b₂ : B).

  Section InvertibleToCartesian.
    Context {a : B}
            {f g : a --> b₁ ⊗ b₂}
            (α : f ==> g)
            (Hα : is_invertible_2cell (α ▹ π₂)).

    
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, a: B
f, g: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
α: f ==> g
Hα: is_invertible_2cell (α ▹ π₂)
h: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
β: h ==> g
δp: h · π₁ ==> f · π₁
q: β ▹ π₁ = δp • (α ▹ π₁)
isaprop (∑ δ : h ==> f, δ ▹ π₁ = δp × δ • α = β)

    
B: bicat_with_binprod

isProofIrrelevant
  (∑ δ : h ==> f, δ ▹ π₁ = δp × δ • α = β)

φ₁ = φ₂

B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, a: B
f, g: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
α: f ==> g
Hα: is_invertible_2cell (α ▹ π₂)
h: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
β: h ==> g
δp: h · π₁ ==> f · π₁
q: β ▹ π₁ = δp • (α ▹ π₁)
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ δ : h ==> f, δ ▹ π₁ = δp × δ • α = β
(pr1 φ₁ ▹ binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)))
• (α ▹ π₂) =
(pr1 φ₂ ▹ binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)))
• (α ▹ π₂)

        
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, a: B
f, g: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
α: f ==> g
Hα: is_invertible_2cell (α ▹ π₂)
h: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
β: h ==> g
δp: h · π₁ ==> f · π₁
q: β ▹ π₁ = δp • (α ▹ π₁)
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ δ : h ==> f, δ ▹ π₁ = δp × δ • α = β
(pr1 φ₁ • α) ▹ π₂ = (pr1 φ₂ • α) ▹ π₂

        
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, a: B
f, g: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
α: f ==> g
Hα: is_invertible_2cell (α ▹ π₂)

q: β ▹ π₁ = δp • (α ▹ π₁)
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ δ : h ==> f, δ ▹ π₁ = δp × δ • α = β
pr1 φ₁ • α = pr1 φ₂ • α

        exact (pr22 φ₁ @ !(pr22 φ₂)).
    Qed.

   (let X := λ b₁ b₂ : pr1 B, pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂) in
    X b₁ b₂) δp ((β ▹ π₂) • Hα ^-1) • α)
▹ binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) =
β ▹ binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
 abstract
              (rewrite <- !rwhisker_vcomp ;
               rewrite binprod_ump_2cell_pr1 ;
               exact (!q)).
          
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, a: B
f, g: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
α: f ==> g
Hα: is_invertible_2cell (α ▹ π₂)
h: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
β: h ==> g
δp: h · π₁ ==> f · π₁
q: β ▹ π₁ = δp • (α ▹ π₁)
(binprod_ump_2cell
   (let X := λ b₁ b₂ : pr1 B, pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂) in
    X b₁ b₂) δp ((β ▹ π₂) • Hα ^-1) • α)
▹ binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) =
β ▹ binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
 abstract
              (rewrite <- !rwhisker_vcomp ;
               rewrite binprod_ump_2cell_pr2 ;
               rewrite !vassocl ;
               refine (_ @ id2_right _) ;
               rewrite vcomp_linv ;
               apply idpath).
    Defined.
  End InvertibleToCartesian.

  Section CartesianToInvertible.
    Context {a : B}
            {f g : a --> b₁ ⊗ b₂}
            (α : f ==> g)
            (Hα : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib π₁ α).

    Let h : a --> b₁ ⊗ b₂ := ⟨ f · π₁, g · π₂ ⟩.
    Let δ : h ==> g
      := binprod_ump_2cell
           (pr2 (pr2 B _ _))
           (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 _ _ _ _ • (α ▹ _))
           (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 _ _ _ _).
    Let hπ₁ : h · π₁ ==> f · π₁ := binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 _ _ _ _.

    
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, a: B
f, g: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
α: f ==> g
Hα: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib π₁ α
h:= ⟨ f · π₁, g · π₂ ⟩: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
δ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
     a (f · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))
     (g · binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))
   • (α ▹ binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))))
  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
     a (f · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))
     (g · binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))): h ==> g
hπ₁:= binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
  a (f · π₁) (g · π₂): h · π₁ ==> f · π₁
δ ▹ π₁ = hπ₁ • (α ▹ π₁)

    
B: bicat_with_binprod

  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))

     (g · binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))
   • (α ▹ binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))))
  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
     a (f · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))
     (g · binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))): h ==> g

δ ▹ π₁ = hπ₁ • (α ▹ π₁)

      apply binprod_ump_2cell_pr1.
    Qed.

    Let lift : ∃! δ0 : h ==> f, δ0 ▹ π₁ = hπ₁ × δ0 • α = δ
      := Hα h δ hπ₁ cartesian_to_invertible_eq.
    Let lift_map : h ==> f := pr11 lift.
    Let inv : g · π₂ ==> f · π₂
      := (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 _ _ _ _)^-1 • (lift_map ▹ π₂).

    Let ζ : f ==> f
      := binprod_ump_2cell
           (pr2 (pr2 B _ _))
           (id2 _)
           ((α ▹ π₂) • inv).

    
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, a: B
f, g: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
α: f ==> g
Hα: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib π₁ α
h:= ⟨ f · π₁, g · π₂ ⟩: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
δ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
     a (f · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))
     (g · binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))
   • (α ▹ binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))))
  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
     a (f · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))
     (g · binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))): h ==> g
hπ₁:= binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
  a (f · π₁) (g · π₂): h · π₁ ==> f · π₁
lift:= Hα h δ hπ₁ cartesian_to_invertible_eq: ∃! δ0 : h ==> f, δ0 ▹ π₁ = hπ₁ × δ0 • α = δ
lift_map:= pr11 lift: h ==> f
inv:= (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
   a (f · π₁) (g · π₂)) ^-1 • 
(lift_map ▹ π₂): g · π₂ ==> f · π₂
ζ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  (id₂ (f · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))))
  ((α ▹ π₂) • inv): f ==> f
ζ = id₂ f

   a (f · π₁) (g · π₂)) ^-1 • 
(lift_map ▹ π₂): g · π₂ ==> f · π₂
ζ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  (id₂ (f · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))))
  ((α ▹ π₂) • inv): f ==> f
(ζ • α) ▹ binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) =
α ▹ binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, a: B
f, g: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
α: f ==> g
Hα: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib π₁ α
h:= ⟨ f · π₁, g · π₂ ⟩: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
δ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 
     (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a
     (f · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))
     (g · binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))
   • (α ▹ binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))))
  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 
     (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a
     (f · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))
     (g · binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))): h ==> g
hπ₁:= binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
  a (f · π₁) (g · π₂): h · π₁ ==> f · π₁
lift:= Hα h δ hπ₁ cartesian_to_invertible_eq: ∃! δ0 : h ==> f, δ0 ▹ π₁ = hπ₁ × δ0 • α = δ
lift_map:= pr11 lift: h ==> f
inv:= (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
   a (f · π₁) (g · π₂)) ^-1 • 
(lift_map ▹ π₂): g · π₂ ==> f · π₂
ζ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  (id₂ (f · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))))
  ((α ▹ π₂) • inv): f ==> f
(ζ • α) ▹ binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) =
α ▹ binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))

• ((binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a
      (f · π₁) (g · π₂)) ^-1

  (id₂ (f · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))))

id₂ f • α = α
 apply id2_left.
    Qed.

    
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, a: B
f, g: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
α: f ==> g
Hα: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib π₁ α
h:= ⟨ f · π₁, g · π₂ ⟩: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
δ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
     a (f · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))
     (g · binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))
   • (α ▹ binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))))
  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
     a (f · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))
     (g · binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))): h ==> g
hπ₁:= binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
  a (f · π₁) (g · π₂): h · π₁ ==> f · π₁
lift:= Hα h δ hπ₁ cartesian_to_invertible_eq: ∃! δ0 : h ==> f, δ0 ▹ π₁ = hπ₁ × δ0 • α = δ
lift_map:= pr11 lift: h ==> f
inv:= (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
   a (f · π₁) (g · π₂)) ^-1 • 
(lift_map ▹ π₂): g · π₂ ==> f · π₂
ζ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  (id₂ (f · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))))
  ((α ▹ π₂) • inv): f ==> f
(α ▹ π₂) • inv = id₂ (f · π₂)

B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, a: B
f, g: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
α: f ==> g
Hα: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib π₁ α
h:= ⟨ f · π₁, g · π₂ ⟩: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
δ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
     a (f · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))
     (g · binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))
   • (α ▹ binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))))
  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
     a (f · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))
     (g · binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂)))): h ==> g
hπ₁:= binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
  a (f · π₁) (g · π₂): h · π₁ ==> f · π₁
lift:= Hα h δ hπ₁ cartesian_to_invertible_eq: ∃! δ0 : h ==> f, δ0 ▹ π₁ = hπ₁ × δ0 • α = δ
lift_map:= pr11 lift: h ==> f
inv:= (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
   a (f · π₁) (g · π₂)) ^-1 • 
(lift_map ▹ π₂): g · π₂ ==> f · π₂
ζ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  (id₂ (f · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))))
  ((α ▹ π₂) • inv): f ==> f
(binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a
   (f · π₁) (g · π₂)) ^-1 • ((lift_map • α) ▹ π₂) =
id₂ (g · π₂)

        apply binprod_ump_2cell_pr2.

(β : invertible_2cell (h · π₁) f),
is_cartesian_2cell_sfib π₁ γ × γ ▹ π₁ = β • α

B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, a: B
f: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⟧
g: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
α: f ==> g · π₁
(⟪ α, id₂ (g · π₂) ⟫ • prod_1cell_eta_map B g) ▹ π₁ =
prod_1cell_pr1 B f (g · π₂) • α
 abstract
        (unfold prod_1cell_eta_map ;
         rewrite <- !rwhisker_vcomp ;
         etrans ;
         [ apply maponpaths ;
           apply binprod_ump_2cell_pr1
         | ] ;
         rewrite prod_2cell_pr1 ;
         rewrite !vassocl ;
         rewrite vcomp_linv ;
         rewrite id2_right ;
         apply idpath).
  Defined.

b₁, b₂, x, y: B

B: bicat_with_binprod

h: B ⟦ y, x ⟧
f, g: B ⟦ x, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
γ: f ==> g

i:= cartesian_to_invertible γ Hγ: is_invertible_2cell (γ ▹ π₂)
rassociator h g π₂ • ((h ◃ i ^-1) • (h ◃ (γ ▹ π₂))) =
rassociator h g π₂

      
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, x, y: B
h: B ⟦ y, x ⟧
f, g: B ⟦ x, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
γ: f ==> g
Hγ: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib π₁ γ
i:= cartesian_to_invertible γ Hγ: is_invertible_2cell (γ ▹ π₂)
rassociator h g π₂ • (h ◃ (i ^-1 • (γ ▹ π₂))) =
rassociator h g π₂

      
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, x, y: B
h: B ⟦ y, x ⟧
f, g: B ⟦ x, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
γ: f ==> g
Hγ: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib π₁ γ
i:= cartesian_to_invertible γ Hγ: is_invertible_2cell (γ ▹ π₂)
rassociator h g π₂ • (h ◃ id₂ (g · π₂)) =
rassociator h g π₂

      
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, x, y: B
h: B ⟦ y, x ⟧
f, g: B ⟦ x, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
γ: f ==> g
Hγ: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib π₁ γ
i:= cartesian_to_invertible γ Hγ: is_invertible_2cell (γ ▹ π₂)
rassociator h g π₂ • id₂ (h · (g · π₂)) =
rassociator h g π₂

      apply id2_right.
  Qed.

End ProjectionSFib.

(**
 2. First projection is a Street opfibration
 *)
Section ProjectionSOpFib.
  Context {B : bicat_with_binprod}
          (b₁ b₂ : B).

  Section InvertibleToOpCartesian.
    Context {a : B}
            {f g : a --> b₁ ⊗ b₂}
            (α : f ==> g)
            (Hα : is_invertible_2cell (α ▹ π₂)).

    
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, a: B
f, g: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
α: f ==> g
Hα: is_invertible_2cell (α ▹ π₂)
h: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
β: f ==> h
δp: g · π₁ ==> h · π₁
q: β ▹ π₁ = (α ▹ π₁) • δp
isaprop (∑ δ : g ==> h, δ ▹ π₁ = δp × α • δ = β)

isaprop (∑ δ : g ==> h, δ ▹ π₁ = δp × α • δ = β)

  End InvertibleToOpCartesian.

  Section OpCartesianToInvertible.
    Context {a : B}
            {f g : a --> b₁ ⊗ b₂}
            (α : f ==> g)
            (Hα : is_opcartesian_2cell_sopfib π₁ α).

    Let h : a --> b₁ ⊗ b₂ := ⟨ g · π₁, f · π₂ ⟩.
    Let δ : f ==> h
      := binprod_ump_2cell
           (pr2 (pr2 B _ _))
           (α ▹ _ • (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 _ _ (g · π₁) (f · π₂))^-1)
           ((binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 _ _ (g · π₁) (f · π₂))^-1).
    Let hπ₁ : g · π₁ ==> h · π₁
      := (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 _ _ (g · π₁) (f · π₂))^-1.

    
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, a: B
f, g: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
α: f ==> g
Hα: is_opcartesian_2cell_sopfib π₁ α
h:= ⟨ g · π₁, f · π₂ ⟩: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
δ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  ((α ▹ π₁)
   • (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1
        (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a (g · π₁)
        (f · π₂)) ^-1)
  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
     a (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) ^-1: f ==> h
hπ₁:= (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
   a (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) ^-1: g · π₁ ==> h · π₁
δ ▹ π₁ = (α ▹ π₁) • hπ₁

    
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, a: B
f, g: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
α: f ==> g
Hα: is_opcartesian_2cell_sopfib π₁ α
h:= ⟨ g · π₁, f · π₂ ⟩: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
δ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  ((α ▹ π₁)
   • (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1
        (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a (g · π₁)
        (f · π₂)) ^-1)
  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
     a (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) ^-1: f ==> h
hπ₁:= (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
   a (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) ^-1: g · π₁ ==> h · π₁
δ ▹ π₁ = (α ▹ π₁) • hπ₁

      apply binprod_ump_2cell_pr1.
    Qed.

    Let lift : ∃! (δ0 : g ==> h), δ0 ▹ π₁ = hπ₁ × α • δ0 = δ
      := Hα h δ hπ₁ opcartesian_to_invertible_eq.
    Let lift_map : g ==> h := pr11 lift.
    Let inv : g · π₂ ==> f · π₂
      := lift_map ▹ π₂ • binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 _ _ _ _.

    Let ζ : g ==> g
      := binprod_ump_2cell
           (pr2 (pr2 B _ _))
           (id2 _)
           (inv • (α ▹ π₂)).

    
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, a: B
f, g: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
α: f ==> g
Hα: is_opcartesian_2cell_sopfib π₁ α
h:= ⟨ g · π₁, f · π₂ ⟩: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
δ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  ((α ▹ π₁)
   • (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1
        (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a (g · π₁)
        (f · π₂)) ^-1)
  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
     a (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) ^-1: f ==> h
hπ₁:= (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
   a (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) ^-1: g · π₁ ==> h · π₁
lift:= Hα h δ hπ₁ opcartesian_to_invertible_eq: ∃! δ0 : g ==> h, δ0 ▹ π₁ = hπ₁ × α • δ0 = δ
lift_map:= pr11 lift: g ==> h
inv:= (lift_map ▹ π₂)
• binprod_ump_1cell_pr2
    (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a 
    (g · π₁) (f · π₂): g · π₂ ==> f · π₂
ζ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  (id₂ (g · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))))
  (inv • (α ▹ π₂)): g ==> g
ζ = id₂ g

    
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, a: B
f, g: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
α: f ==> g
Hα: is_opcartesian_2cell_sopfib π₁ α
h:= ⟨ g · π₁, f · π₂ ⟩: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
δ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  ((α ▹ π₁)
   • (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1
        (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a (g · π₁)
        (f · π₂)) ^-1)
  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
     a (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) ^-1: f ==> h
hπ₁:= (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
   a (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) ^-1: g · π₁ ==> h · π₁
lift:= Hα h δ hπ₁ opcartesian_to_invertible_eq: ∃! δ0 : g ==> h, δ0 ▹ π₁ = hπ₁ × α • δ0 = δ
lift_map:= pr11 lift: g ==> h
inv:= (lift_map ▹ π₂)

inv:= (lift_map ▹ π₂)

B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, a: B
f, g: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
α: f ==> g
Hα: is_opcartesian_2cell_sopfib π₁ α
h:= ⟨ g · π₁, f · π₂ ⟩: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
δ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  ((α ▹ π₁)
   • (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1
        (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a (g · π₁)
        (f · π₂)) ^-1)
  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
     a (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) ^-1: f ==> h
hπ₁:= (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
   a (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) ^-1: g · π₁ ==> h · π₁
lift:= Hα h δ hπ₁ opcartesian_to_invertible_eq: ∃! δ0 : g ==> h, δ0 ▹ π₁ = hπ₁ × α • δ0 = δ
lift_map:= pr11 lift: g ==> h
inv:= (lift_map ▹ π₂)
• binprod_ump_1cell_pr2
    (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a 
    (g · π₁) (f · π₂): g · π₂ ==> f · π₂
ζ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  (id₂ (g · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))))
  (inv • (α ▹ π₂)): g ==> g
((δ ▹ π₂)
 • binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a
     (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) • (α ▹ π₂) =
α ▹ binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))

    (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a

((binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))

       a (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) ^-1 ▹ π₂)

     (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) • (α ▹ π₂) =

        (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a (g · π₁)
        (f · π₂)) ^-1)

     a (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) ^-1: f ==> h

  ((α ▹ π₁)
   • (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1
        (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a (g · π₁)
        (f · π₂)) ^-1)

     a (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) ^-1: f ==> h

 apply id2_rwhisker.

 apply id2_right.

   a (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) ^-1: g · π₁ ==> h · π₁
lift:= Hα h δ hπ₁ opcartesian_to_invertible_eq: ∃! δ0 : g ==> h, δ0 ▹ π₁ = hπ₁ × α • δ0 = δ
lift_map:= pr11 lift: g ==> h
inv:= (lift_map ▹ π₂)

δ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  ((α ▹ π₁)
   • (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1
        (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a (g · π₁)
        (f · π₂)) ^-1)
  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
     a (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) ^-1: f ==> h
hπ₁:= (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
   a (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) ^-1: g · π₁ ==> h · π₁
lift:= Hα h δ hπ₁ opcartesian_to_invertible_eq: ∃! δ0 : g ==> h, δ0 ▹ π₁ = hπ₁ × α • δ0 = δ
lift_map:= pr11 lift: g ==> h
inv:= (lift_map ▹ π₂)

    (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a

  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a

B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, a: B
f, g: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
α: f ==> g
Hα: is_opcartesian_2cell_sopfib π₁ α
h:= ⟨ g · π₁, f · π₂ ⟩: B ⟦ a, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
δ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  ((α ▹ π₁)
   • (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1
        (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a (g · π₁)
        (f · π₂)) ^-1)
  (binprod_ump_1cell_pr2 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
     a (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) ^-1: f ==> h
hπ₁:= (binprod_ump_1cell_pr1 (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂))
   a (g · π₁) (f · π₂)) ^-1: g · π₁ ==> h · π₁
lift:= Hα h δ hπ₁ opcartesian_to_invertible_eq: ∃! δ0 : g ==> h, δ0 ▹ π₁ = hπ₁ × α • δ0 = δ
lift_map:= pr11 lift: g ==> h
inv:= (lift_map ▹ π₂)
• binprod_ump_1cell_pr2
    (pr2 (binprod_of B b₁ b₂)) a 
    (g · π₁) (f · π₂): g · π₂ ==> f · π₂
ζ:= binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))
  (id₂ (g · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))))
  (inv • (α ▹ π₂)): g ==> g
inv • (α ▹ π₂) = id₂ (g · π₂)

lift:= Hα h δ hπ₁ opcartesian_to_invertible_eq: ∃! δ0 : g ==> h, δ0 ▹ π₁ = hπ₁ × α • δ0 = δ
lift_map:= pr11 lift: g ==> h
inv:= (lift_map ▹ π₂)

  (id₂ (g · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (pr2 B b₁ b₂))))
  (inv • (α ▹ π₂)): g ==> g
g · π₂ ==> f · π₂

b₁, b₂, x, y: B
h: B ⟦ y, x ⟧
f, g: B ⟦ x, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
γ: f ==> g
Hγ: is_opcartesian_2cell_sopfib π₁ γ
i:= opcartesian_to_invertible γ Hγ: is_invertible_2cell (γ ▹ π₂)
((rassociator h g π₂ • (h ◃ i ^-1))
 • lassociator h f π₂) • ((h ◃ γ) ▹ π₂) =
id₂ (h · g · π₂)
 
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, x, y: B
h: B ⟦ y, x ⟧
f, g: B ⟦ x, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
γ: f ==> g
Hγ: is_opcartesian_2cell_sopfib π₁ γ
i:= opcartesian_to_invertible γ Hγ: is_invertible_2cell (γ ▹ π₂)
rassociator h g π₂
• ((h ◃ i ^-1) • (lassociator h f π₂ • ((h ◃ γ) ▹ π₂))) =
id₂ (h · g · π₂)

      
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, x, y: B
h: B ⟦ y, x ⟧
f, g: B ⟦ x, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
γ: f ==> g
Hγ: is_opcartesian_2cell_sopfib π₁ γ
i:= opcartesian_to_invertible γ Hγ: is_invertible_2cell (γ ▹ π₂)
rassociator h g π₂
• ((h ◃ i ^-1) • ((h ◃ (γ ▹ π₂)) • lassociator h g π₂)) =
id₂ (h · g · π₂)

      
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, x, y: B
h: B ⟦ y, x ⟧
f, g: B ⟦ x, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
γ: f ==> g
Hγ: is_opcartesian_2cell_sopfib π₁ γ
i:= opcartesian_to_invertible γ Hγ: is_invertible_2cell (γ ▹ π₂)
((rassociator h g π₂ • (h ◃ i ^-1)) • (h ◃ (γ ▹ π₂)))
• lassociator h g π₂ = id₂ (h · g · π₂)

      
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, x, y: B
h: B ⟦ y, x ⟧
f, g: B ⟦ x, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
γ: f ==> g
Hγ: is_opcartesian_2cell_sopfib π₁ γ
i:= opcartesian_to_invertible γ Hγ: is_invertible_2cell (γ ▹ π₂)
((rassociator h g π₂ • (h ◃ i ^-1)) • (h ◃ (γ ▹ π₂)))
• lassociator h g π₂ =
rassociator h g π₂ • lassociator h g π₂

      
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, x, y: B
h: B ⟦ y, x ⟧
f, g: B ⟦ x, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
γ: f ==> g
Hγ: is_opcartesian_2cell_sopfib π₁ γ
i:= opcartesian_to_invertible γ Hγ: is_invertible_2cell (γ ▹ π₂)
(rassociator h g π₂ • (h ◃ i ^-1)) • (h ◃ (γ ▹ π₂)) =
rassociator h g π₂

      
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, x, y: B
h: B ⟦ y, x ⟧
f, g: B ⟦ x, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
γ: f ==> g
Hγ: is_opcartesian_2cell_sopfib π₁ γ
i:= opcartesian_to_invertible γ Hγ: is_invertible_2cell (γ ▹ π₂)
rassociator h g π₂ • ((h ◃ i ^-1) • (h ◃ (γ ▹ π₂))) =
rassociator h g π₂

      
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, x, y: B
h: B ⟦ y, x ⟧
f, g: B ⟦ x, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
γ: f ==> g
Hγ: is_opcartesian_2cell_sopfib π₁ γ
i:= opcartesian_to_invertible γ Hγ: is_invertible_2cell (γ ▹ π₂)
rassociator h g π₂ • (h ◃ (i ^-1 • (γ ▹ π₂))) =
rassociator h g π₂

      
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, x, y: B
h: B ⟦ y, x ⟧
f, g: B ⟦ x, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
γ: f ==> g
Hγ: is_opcartesian_2cell_sopfib π₁ γ
i:= opcartesian_to_invertible γ Hγ: is_invertible_2cell (γ ▹ π₂)
rassociator h g π₂ • (h ◃ id₂ (g · π₂)) =
rassociator h g π₂

      
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂, x, y: B
h: B ⟦ y, x ⟧
f, g: B ⟦ x, b₁ ⊗ b₂ ⟧
γ: f ==> g
Hγ: is_opcartesian_2cell_sopfib π₁ γ
i:= opcartesian_to_invertible γ Hγ: is_invertible_2cell (γ ▹ π₂)
rassociator h g π₂ • id₂ (h · (g · π₂)) =
rassociator h g π₂

      apply id2_right.
  Qed.

b₁, b₂: B
internal_sopfib (π₁ : B ⟦ b₁ ⊗ b₂, b₁ ⟧)

 exact pr1_internal_opcleaving.
